	// Rewrite of the Phantom Assassin Phantom Strike ability
	// Author: Pizzalol
	// Date: 29.09.2015.
	"stareclipse"
	{
		// General
		// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"BaseClass"	"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityTextureName"	"icon\stareclipse_ability"
		"AbilityBehavior"	"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_UNIT_TARGET | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_IGNORE_BACKSWING"
		"AbilityUnitTargetType"	"DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_HERO | DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_BASIC"
		"AbilityUnitTargetTeam"	"DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_TEAM_ENEMY"
		"SpellImmunityType"	"SPELL_IMMUNITY_ENEMIES_YES"
		"CastFilterRejectCaster"	"1"
		"FightRecapLevel"	"1"
		"HotKeyOverride"	"D"
		"AbilityCastPoint"	"0.3 0.3 0.3 0.3"
		// Time
		// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilityCooldown"	"18 15 12 9"
		// Cost
		// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilityManaCost"	"90 90 90 90"

		// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilityCastRange"	"1000 1000 1000 1000"
		"precache"
		{
			"particle"	"particles/units/heroes/kuroyuki/sven_spell_great_cleave.vpcf"
		}
		"OnUpgrade"
		{
			"RunScript"
			{
				"ScriptFile"	"heroes/hero_kuroyuki/kuroyuki.lua"
				"Function"	"LevelUpAbility"
				"ability_name"	"bluemodel"
			}
		}
		"OnSpellStart"
		{
			"Blink"
			{
				"Target"	"TARGET"
			}
			"RunScript"
			{
				"ScriptFile"	"heroes/hero_phantom_assassin/phantom_strike.lua"
				"Function"	"stareclipseMotion"
				"Target"	"TARGET"
				"stareclipse_modifier"	"stareclipse_modifier"
			}
			"ApplyModifier"
			{
				"Target"	"CASTER"
				"ModifierName"	"stareclipse_modifier"
			}
		}
		"Modifiers"
		{
			"stareclipse_modifier"
			{
				"IsBuff"	"1"
				// "%attack_damage" is set to the damage value before mitigation
				"OnAttackLanded"
				{
					"CleaveAttack"
					{
						"CleavePercent"	"%star_eclipse_damage"
						"CleaveRadius"	"%star_eclipse_radius"
						"CleaveEffect"	"particles/units/heroes/kuroyuki/sven_spell_great_cleave.vpcf"
					}
				}
				"Properties"
				{
					"MODIFIER_PROPERTY_ATTACKSPEED_BONUS_CONSTANT"	"%bonus_attack_speed"
				}
				"Duration"	"%time"
			}
			"modifier_stareclipse"
			{
				"Attributes"	"MODIFIER_ATTRIBUTE_PERMANENT | MODIFIER_ATTRIBUTE_IGNORE_INVULNERABLE"
				"Passive"	"1"
				"OnIntervalThink"
				{
					"RunScript"
					{
						"Target"	"CASTER"
						"Function"	"kuroyukicheck2"
						"ScriptFile"	"scripts/vscripts/heroes/hero_kuroyuki/kuroyuki.lua"
					}
				}
				"ThinkInterval"	"0.03"
				"IsHidden"	"1"
			}
		}

		// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilityValues"
		{
